"726","CYLENTIUM INC","WAYNE RONHAAR","","512 COUNTY ROAD 140","","BURNET","TX","78611-2997","Cylentium Inc., is a leading provider of security software for wireless, ethernet, and Cyber Security networks. Cylentium Systems has deep experience in securing network communications over the close and extended distances via IEEE 802.16 and IEEE 802.16d, while maintaining the superior performance of a wireless broadband wide area network. Unlike virtual private network (VPN)—based systems, Cylentium’s Cylent encrypts full Ethernet frames, rather than just IP payloads, hiding vital information such as IP addresses, applications, and ports from unauthorized listeners. Frame-level encryption also protects non-data network traffic, including Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) requests or ARP messages, from being compromised and used to attack the network. Cylentium is a robust, FIPS 140—2 certified wireless security software solution that enables government agencies,and enterprises the productivity benefits of wireless networks while minimizing security risks.","wayne@cylentium.com","www.cylentium.com"

Cuff-based methods are susceptible to operator error, causing inaccuracies leading to hypertension misdiagnosis and discordant medication prescriptions. In contrast, arterial monitoring is highly accurate but invasive, expensive, and restricted to specialized settings. Clinicians need a low-cost way to combine the best of arterial monitoring’s accurate, real-time, and continuous view of blood pressure with the non-invasive, low-risk accessibility of cuff-based methods.","ben@emx.bio",""
